--- File: ./Campaigns/Campaign 1/Chronicles/Entry 15.md ---

**Day 12 (continued)**

The group continues to approach Arcadia, wandering stealthily through the forest. Theren senses necromancy getting stronger as they approach the city. There is no secret here – the necromancy is not hidden. They spot guards on the walls and some patrolling outside the city limits. Temerity suggests capturing a guard so that he can impersonate one. Lavender agrees with the plan. They all agree that heading to a smaller gate makes more sense than approaching the main gate.

Lavender tries to make a lasso with which to ensnare a guard, but her gauntlets are too cumbersome. She becomes more and more frustrated and a cold fire burns within her. As the power surges within her, she glows blue with rage. Temerity sees this and moves to assist, but then tries to tie her up. He grabs the rope but it’s snagged in her gauntlet. Aurius helps him to run it round and round Lavender. Chikatika helps to tie the knot. Theren demands to know what Temerity is doing and he declares that Lavender will kill when she gets free.

Temerity places Korako on Lavender’s lap to try and calm her. He declares the rabbit a relaxation aid. However, Korako is unsettled and doesn’t want to be there. Lavender’s prodigious strength tears through the rope thread by thread. She lunges at Temerity, who escapes up a nearby tree. Korako is left abandoned on the floor feeling unsafe. Temerity leaps back down to rescue him. Lavender falls flat on her face as she trips, but fresh snow appears to form up and break her fall. Temerity retrieves Korako and then walks casually over to Lavender and offers her a hand. She tries to pull him down to the floor. He ends up being flipper over her and splats in the snow, winded. Korako is hastily tossed to Chikatika, who takes care of him.

The shenanigans have drawn the attention of a group of guards. Lavender sees them and fires her crossbow at them, but the bolt goes wide, alerting the guards. She fires again and hits the scout at the head of the group, badly wounding him. The scout returns fire and wings Lavender. Unexpectedly, an arrow shoots out of the trees and thuds into the scout’s shoulder. Lavender draws her sword and charges at the other two guards as the scout veils himself from detection. The first guard’s breastplate is shattered from shoulder to spleen and his corpse drops to the ground. The second guard has his head cleaved off.

The party hears a thud behind them as someone jumps down from a tree and dashes past them. It is a rock gnome. He is dirty and covered in moss, but very fast. He skewers a guard with his rapier. Theren tries to use hideous laughter to incapacitate the scout, very aware that capturing one alive will gain them information. However, it fails. He shouts to take the scout alive. Temerity tries to charm the scout but that too fails. The scout veils himself again and attacks the rock gnome with hit short daggers, causing minor damage. The scout tries to retreat up a tree but is wounded and falls on his arse.

The rock gnome re-enters the tree line and conceals himself. Lavender runs over to the prone scout and slams her sword down repeatedly into the guard, leaving a pulped mess at the base of the tree. Eventually her strikes slow and she returns to her senses. Silence settles and her raspy breathing echoes through the trees. Temerity saunters up and praises her blood-spattered form. Theren heads to the beheaded guard but notices that the armour is not a uniform and would therefore be useless as a disguise. He loots a shortsword instead.

The rock gnome reappears. He is Gage Greengather. He heads to the gate. Temerity thinks he is suspicious but Theren insists that he is a friend, which leads to some unhelpful bickering.

Lavender is annoyed with Temerity. She looks guiltily down at the bodies of the guards. She feels that they should bury the bodies. Temerity asks Gage if he has anything to help with digging. Gage says nothing but wanders into the forest in search of fungus. However, the necromantic magic has decimated life in the area. Temerity and Theren also look around, but the area is utterly dead. When they return, Guido has started gnawing on one of the guards. Lavender moves the bodies into the bushes and Theren uses prestidigitation to remove the bloodstains from the floor. Temerity feels odd for having caused the situation in the first place and feels concerned about leaving corpses in a necromantic area. He helps Lavender to move the bodies and stares at them. Lavender suggests burning them, but Temerity’s eyes begin to change. Green root-lie accents appear in his the deep gold. Chikatika bounds onto his shoulder. The green radiance spreads to her. Her eyes glow and the power ignites, descending from the sky and immolating the pile of corpses. The bodies had already been tainted by the necromantic energy permeating the area but have now burned to ash that blows away on the wind.

Theren is watching Gage, who stands apart from the group, while Lavender and Temerity oversee the cremation. Gage speaks, informing them that he knows a way into the city – there are gaps in the fence. Theren asks if these gaps could accommodate Lavender’s not inconsiderable size. Gage cannot be certain. Lavender tries to jolt Temerity from his reverie while Gage and Theren plan to infiltrate the city. Lavender wants to wait until cover of darkness but it is still morning. Theren asks Gage what he knows about the city. He replies that Lavender might be questioned if she appeared in the city, but that Theren and Temerity would probably be innocuous. Gage mentions that he was tasked with keeping an eye on Lavender.

Temerity is alert and uses detect thoughts on Gage. The rock gnome wants to help but is in the employ of the necromancers. His mind is methodical and ordered. He also reads Lavender’s and finds that she is occupied with thoughts of her brother, Orris. She suspects that he is here but on the wrong side. Orris has been her motivation from the start. Lavender rests her hand on her sword hilt and asks Gage if there’s anything else he wants to say. Gage’s face is implacable. Theren asks him why he wants to help. He puts his cards on the table: he is a mercenary who was in the employ of the necromancers. However, he sees the effect of the necromancers on the people around them and wants nothing more to do with their schemes. He has been watching the party for a while and has decided to throw his lot in with them instead, seeing in them the potential to stop the threat of the necromancers. Lavender asks him where Orris is. Gage repeats that his task was to watch her. Lavender says that they have little choice in the matter. She tries to gain Temerity’s attention. He asks Chikatika her opinion. She scratches her head, chunters and shrugs. Temerity returns to himself and compliments Chikatika.

Gage starts walking, with Theren following. Lavender also leaves to follow them. Temerity tries to stop her but fails. He follows also and overtakes them all to speak to Gage. He asks if the gnome will make a clockwork rabbit. Gage discusses the practicalities and eventually agrees.

They avoid the guards by walking just beyond the treeline. There are towers but they look over the roads and exits. Temerity tries to make small talk with Gage but he is not very receptive. The party struggles to keep up with him as he moves stealthily through the trees. They reach a part of the wall that looks normal but Gage informs them that there is a secret opening there. Temerity spots a black cat on top of the wall but it is too far away. Theren offers to bring it down but Temerity declines. Gage goes through the secret entrance with Theren following. They both move stealthily through the city. Lavender watches for guards and tries to avoid talking to Temerity about the glowing they both experienced during the scuffle with the guards.

Within the city, everything functions normally but it feels awkward. Gage heads for a specific place and Theren follows. They arrive at an inn where Gage knows the bartender, someone who has done favours for him before. He negotiates with the bartender, asking to get his new friends into the city. The bartender agrees, but needs a flower to save his daughter from a disease. The bartender agrees to defer the payment of the flower in return for 30 gold pieces. He will refund half when they bring him the flower. He promises them a 15 minute window at the east gate without guards. Gage and Theren leave quickly.

Lavender leaves Temerity standing guard at the secret entrance and heads off to check the east gate. After a few minutes of walking, she reaches the east gate and the guards are murmuring about her. Temerity waits until she is out of range and then follows her. Suddenly, a big explosion out in the desiccated forest distracts the guards and Lavender watches them rush off to investigate. She receives a telepathic message from Gage to move in. Temerity creates an illusion on the path of a giant Korako. The one remaining guard at the gate questions the rabbit at spearpoint. The illusion beckons the guard. Runcible grabs the spear and distracts the guard. He manages to lift the guard off the floor slightly and drag him forwards. Whilst this set of distractions takes place, Lavender and Temerity sneak through the gate. Runcible releases the spear and he drops to the ground with a bump. Gage telepathically warns the guard that no-one will believe him if he mentions this. The guard faints and the party heads off.

Temerity rushes to loot the guard but he only has a spear. Temerity doesn’t take it but instead jabs it into the gate hinges high up so that the guard cannot retrieve it. Gage suggests that Lavender is too conspicuous so Theren passes her his cloak. At the inn, Temerity uses his disguise kit to make her more incognito. He dyes her hair red while Theren discusses strategy with Gage. They discuss luring a member of the necromancers’ leadership to the city. There are not as many guards as they expected but it is difficult to know how many necromancers are in the city. They dismiss the idea of interrogating a necromancer. They discuss instead getting information about the numbers and activities of the necromancers. Lavender asks about events or rituals but Gage has limited information about these things. They discount a disinformation campaign and instead discuss an infiltrated assault on the mayor’s residence at night. Gage mentions a distraction and Lavender volunteers. Temerity finishes her disguise.

Gage mentions his debt to the innkeeper. They agree to leave Lavender at the inn as she is too well-known, even with a disguise. Theren agrees to accompany Gage. He leaves behind a schematic for a clockwork rabbit. Temerity agrees to recon. Guido is sent out to gather information while Temerity works the inn, playing music. Lavender meditates and feels a moment of calm. Patterns of ice rise up the window and refract the light into rainbows. It begins to snow in the room and a voice speaks to her. Auriel is pleased with Lavender and tells her that her recent abilities come from her commitment – to the cause, to her companions and to Auriel. The goddess pledges that Lavender can call on her whenever she chooses.

Gage and There head off and discuss who they are. Gage is ex-military and now a mercenary. He grew up in a forest enclave, far from the necromancers. He was used in a recon team as their spy network. Gage has always lived under the yoke of the necromancers. Theren asked what caused him to change his mind. Gage discusses going out on recon with his older brother, who began to change his perceptions. Gage wants to free his people and thinks of himself as a freedom fighter. Theren discusses his past and his new connection with the party, which he doesn’t fully understand. The pair bond well. Gage spots a small handful of the sought-after flowers. They both know that these flowers only grow where blood has been spilled and will not be easy to obtain. Theren senses magic from the flowers – they are strongly guarded. While Theren and Runcible stand guard, Gage goes to harvest the flower but notices that the colour seems to change. He begins o dig out one of the plants but accidentally knocks another flower, causing a puff of iridescent smoke to emerge. The forest around him fills with dire wolves. Gage wants to race up a tree but is rooted to the spot. The dire wolves begin to stalk towards him. He readies his rapier. One of the dire wolves lunges at him and he snaps out of it, finding himself lying on his back screaming, staring up at the canopy. Theren takes over and collects several of the flowers using his herbalism kit. They head back to Arcadia and hand over the flower to the bartender. Theren scoops up the 15 returned gold.

--- File: ./Campaigns/Campaign 1/Chronicles/Entry 16.md ---

**Day 12 (continued)**

Guido returns to the bar dragging a bottle of mead with his tail. Temerity creates a diversion to hide his entrance. He conjures the illusion of lines of tap-dancing rats with gold waistcoats. Everyone falls silent and watches the incredible display of bardic phantasmagoria. Under the cover of this distracting illusion, Temerity scoops up Guido and begins to juggle with him. Temerity pops the cork of the bottle, catches the lute that he was also juggling, strums the final chord and catches the bottle upright on the top of his head. Guido lands head first in the bottle. The audience provides rapturous applause. Various items are thrown at Temerity, mostly gold but the odd item of underwear also. The rats scurry off and the inn returns to normal in the wake of the spectacle. Temerity gathers up 110 gold pieces. The innkeeper is so impressed that he offers Temerity a permanent position at the bar. Temerity instead buys a round of drinks for all present.

Two young gnomes approach and ask him to teach them the illusion magic. However, during the conversation, they notice that Guido is, in fact, real and not an illusion. They begin to suspect Temerity. In an attempt to distract the gnomes, Temerity creates the illusion of flowers growing from Guido’s anus. He tries to sneak the bottle into his bag, but one of the gnomes grabs it. Theren, watching from the bar, sees that the situation is getting out of hand and sends Runcible to retrieve the bottle. Runcible fires a burst of flame at the bottom of the bottle, launching Guido out of it to land atop Temerity’s head with singed whiskers.

Temerity continues on his self-destructive rampage and headbutts one of the gnomes. Both gnomes try to punch Temerity but they miss him. Gage sees the ruckus developing and climbs up above the gallery into the rafters in preparation. Temerity addresses the crowd, trying simultaneously to incite them against the gnomes and aggravate the gnomes. Gage moves to position himself directly above Temerity. Theren despairs of the situation and starts drinking the mead, even though he hates it. The crowd begins to become uncomfortable as some of the more inebriated patrons begin to side with Temerity. Theren sidles out of the bar, leaving Temerity to his brawl.

One of the gnomes pulls out a truncheon and smacks Temerity across the kneecap. The other gnome grabs his hand and wrenches it backwards. Temerity creates an illusion of two sheep mating; the sheep have the gnomes’ faces. Lavender is outside listening to the brawl but doesn’t get involved, remembering to remain incognito. Gage aims his bow at the glassware on the bar in an attempt to distract the participants from the brawl. He shoots the glass in the innkeeper’s hand and everyone turns to look. The innkeeper is furious at someone for using weapons in his bar. Gage drops to the floor and attempts to lie his way out of the situation. The gnomes are now staring at Gage, but still try to attack Temerity, failing due to the distraction. Temerity’s illusion shifts now – there are more sheep, one with the face of every gnome in the bar, including Gage. They are all engaged in deviant acts. Temerity is also present in the illusion, standing as a shepherd benevolently watching over his flock. Everyone in the bar stops and stares at the illusion for a worrying amount of time. Silence blankets the place. Theren hears that the ruckus has ended and peeks through the door. He sees the illusion and hastily leaves again. No-one in the bar can tear their eyes away from the disturbing scene.

Just as the illusion fades, the sheep morph fully into the gnomes, link hands with Temerity and bow before winking out of existence. Horrified silence pervades everywhere. Everyone returns to their business, as if pretending that the tableau never existed. Temerity packs away his things, struts over to the bar and plonks down a stack of 10 gold pieces. He then returns to his corner and continues to play his lute. Meanwhile, Guido is frantically searching for something. Temerity tries to entice him over using a glass containing some dregs of beer. However, Guido ignores him and continues his search. Temerity switches tack and sings about liquor under his chair.

Outside, Gage tells Theren that he tried to help in the brawl but that it really didn’t work. Theren passes him the mead bottle. Gage gives it a sniff. It is not local mead but he cannot discern from where it comes. He spots something at the bottom of the bottle but it’s not clear what it is. Theren discusses with Gage about heading to the mayor’s residence and agrees to go. Meanwhile, Lavender waits in her room for the others, wondering what the distraction will be now. Gage remembers to fetch her and throws a small rock at her window. Lavender hears the tink and sees Gage giving her a thumbs-up. She puts up her hood and leaves the inn. Outside, she discusses the plan with Gage.

Theren has sent Runcible on a recon of the mayor’s mansion but he saw nothing of use. Lavender wants to fetch Temerity to provide a distraction. She tells Theren to get Runcible to fetch the bard. Theren tells Runcible to bite Temerity. In the bar, Temerity sees Runcible enter alone and holds out his arm for the dragon. Runcible lands, looking very cross, grabs tightly to Temerity’s arm and pulls. Runcible growls and whips him with his tail, stinging Temerity. The poison doesn’t affect Temerity and he tries to stroke Runcible. The dragon tries to bite Temerity but misses. He flies off.

Temerity stands up, storms over to Guido and picks him up by the scruff. Guido protests vociferously. Temerity taunts Theren outside but Guido’s protests increase and Temerity pays attention. Guido tells Temerity that he found something important but that he lost it in the mead. Theren understands Guido and grabs the mead bottle from Gage. He looks inside but cannot see what Guido is talking about. Temerity sees Theren looking at the mead bottle and sashays over to take the bottle. Theren tries to swing the bottle at him but falls over instead. Lavender grabs the bottle as he falls. Temerity bows elaborately to Lavender and asks graciously for the bottle. Lavender wants to know why. Temerity states that it is Guido who needs the bottle. Lavender inspects it and spots a ring inside.

She empties the mead onto the floor and retrieves the ring. Guido sticks his head beneath the flow and drinks some of the mead; however, he becomes sticky as mead flows over head and bemoans the waste. Lavender tastes the mead from the ends of her fingers. She stares at the ring but senses nothing from it. It is silver with three dark occluded jewels set into it. She shows it to the party. Temerity senses that this is a magical ring and has something to do with necromancy. It glows blue a little bit, like Lavender’s eyes have done in the past. Theren also senses the necromantic energy. He knows how powerful the ring is and that it will require attunement. Someone is already attuned to it and it would be easy for a relative to attune as well. He divines that the ring belongs to Orris and tells Lavender to put the ring on.

Temerity slides the ring onto Lavender’s finger after she removes her gauntlet. Nothing happens, so Theren tells her to meditate upon it, as she should be able to attune to it. He tells her that he believes it is linked to her brother. She returns to the inn.

The rest of the party head to the mayor’s manor. Gage infiltrates from the rear, using perfect stealth skills. Theren remains outside to watch for guards. No-one sees Gage as he ropes up to a balcony and enters the mansion into the servants’ quarters. He investigates the wardrobes and finds clothes. He sends a telepathic message to Theren to come up and disguise himself as a servant. With Runcible’s help, Theren manages to climb up the rope and enter the mansion. He dons a disguise while Gage peeks out of the door and sees the entrance foyer.

Meanwhile, Temerity preens himself before strutting up to the guard at the front door and demanding to entertain the lord, claiming to be the sheep illusionist from the inn. Temerity senses that something is not quite right about this guard. The guard is confused and concerned but is very pale. Snow settles on him but does not melt. Temerity strolls up to the guard and places his hand on the guard’s shoulder, suggesting that they speak inside. The guard looks dead; he stares at Temerity and says nothing. Temerity suggests performing in the courtyard. The guard continues his stony silence. Temerity takes this as consent. Using full vocal projection, he begins to sing a bawdy tavern song, changing some of the lyrics to mention necromancy. The guard begins to sway in time to the music. Theren moves towards a window to listen to Temerity, but he cannot hear what is being sung. Temerity begins banging the front door as part of his performance. The guard continues to sway to the music.

Theren moves away from the window and immediately bumps into another servant. He tries to move around them, but the servant blocks his path. Gage watches this from the shadows. He throws a ball bearing at the servant but the thud is muffled by the carpet. Theren looks up into the face of the servant. The servant is frowning and silent. They appear confused. Theren forces his way past, apologising. The servant stares after Theren but does not move. Gage observes the servant moving off in a different direction to the one they were originally taking before the confrontation. Gage stealthily follows.

Temerity works the words to a knock spell into his song and suddenly there is a massive banging reverberating through the house. The servant stops and turns at the noise. They are near a door that they were about to enter. Gage tackles the servant and knocks them through the door and into some sort of office or study. There is another person in the room – it is his contact, Frolot. Gage brazens it out with Frolot, pretending that the tackle was intentional. Frolot is confused but accepts Gage’s explanation. Gage explains that he was at a bar fight caused by the people he was tasked with tracking. He explains that the one causing all of the noise outside is one of the party and that the other two are still back at the bar. Gage leaves the office after making his report, shutting the door loudly. He puts his ear to the door and listens but no sound comes from within. Gage shrinks back into the shadows.

Temerity opens the main door but does not enter; he projects his voice into the house and begins his sheep illusion. This time all of the sheep are zombies, surrounded by necromancers with hitched up robes who are raping the sheep. The lyrics shift to singing about an undead donkey paladin and his journey of justice across the land.

Theren tries all of the doors along the corridor. The rooms seem unremarkable; everything is unkempt and in a state of disrepair. He enters the library and skims the books. He settles on a section on history and selects a book that seems to be handwritten by the historian of the manor. It is quite old and stops quite abruptly. It talks of things being built and extended. By process of elimination, the manor was extended downwards. He begins to make his way down to find cellar steps.

Back at the inn, Lavender settles onto the floor of her room and meditates on the ring. It is very cold. As she stares into the stones, the occlusion within swirls. She feels not that the ring is cold, but instead an intense absence of heat. She slowly becomes accustomed to the anti-heat. The smoke within the gems pulses in time with her heartbeat. As she attunes to it, she realises that the ring will grant her the ability to use the spirit of death spell. She stares into the gems and within she sees images of this spell being used to strike people down. It is Orris doing the killing. The spirit he has summoned creates the faces of his whole family, including Lavender. Orris raises the fallen and continues the cycle – striking down his enemies and raising their corpses. Cold tears run down Lavender’s cheeks.

Back at the mansion, Gage knows that the true leaders of the outfit must be here, be he has never seen them before. Theren sends Runcible a message to fetch Lavender to join them before they head down into the cellar.

**Day 12 (continued)**

Gage heads to the front door of the mansion to investigate the noise and ends up in the kitchen. The food there looks fairly fresh but the light is dim. The oven is cold, yet some of the food is hot.

Temerity looks at the entrance foyer and sees that it is beautiful and grand. A couple of the servants stop and stare at him vacantly. He continues to sing through the door, weaving his zombie donkey story, but there is still no reaction from the servants.

Theren continues his hunt for the cellar steps. At the end of a long hallway, he sees a dado rail that is not covered in dust, whereas all of the others are dusty. Despite examining the area, he cannot see a way through the wall. He calls Runcible telepathically.

Lavender stands at the front door, listening to Temerity singing. She finds the subject matter mildly concerning. The servants within continue to stare blankly. They show no recognition. Lavender notices that Runcible is trying to lead her, so she moves towards the house and Temerity follows her. One of the servants turns and follows her with its eyes. Lavender becomes rooted to the spot after only having entered the mansion by a couple of steps. Temerity divines that she could be moved by force but is unable to move under her own power.

He continues to sing his song about the zombie donkey paladin, who must now rescue a frozen princess with a kiss. He kisses Lavender and she breaks from the paralysis. She feels rage build within her at this audacious liberty taken and the gall of Temerity but something quells it and tells her that it was necessary. She inclines her head frostily and they follow Runcible.

Gg exits the kitchen and enters the dining room across the corridor. He has been here before, eating with the leaders of the city. He remembers that it was strange how much food there was but that not much of it was touched. He moves stealthily into the dining room, which is completely dark. Using darkvision, he sees that there is no-one in the room with him and the table is unset. Nothing is apparent so he leaves and makes his way back to the main entrance, where he bumps into Temerity and Lavender following Runcible. Gage follows them and provides a rearguard.

They meet Theren at the dead end of the corridor and he points out the strange dado rail. Lavender smacks Temerity to make him shut up, causing mild concussion. Gage doesn’t really recognise this place, even though he’s probably been here before. He knocks on the wall but nothing happens. Theren cannot sense anything magical about this place; Lavender suggests to Temerity that he uses Korako. Korako sniffs at the wall and shudders. He tells his father that it smells bad. Lavender runs her fingers across the panelling of the wall and hears a tiny, constant clicking. She calls Gage over to listen to the clicking; he hears a mechanism, metal tapping on metal, like modified clockwork. Lavender tries shoving the wall but it doesn’t move. Gage tries with the same result.

Gage suddenly notices a grandfather clock nearby. Lavender draws her sword and prepares to attack the wall where the ticking is. Instead, Gage asks Lavender to listen to the clock and compare the ticks. Gage investigates the clock, but he can’t detect what’s going on. Temerity decides to use a direct approach and inserts his rapier into the mechanism to jiggle the lock. Theren listens and can hear that the clock’s ticks match the lock’s. Theren moves the hands to 12 o’clock midnight, but nothing happens. He tries moving the hands to the witching hour and now the door clicks open.

As the massive stone door opens, Temerity’s sword becomes mangled. Try as he might, Temerity cannot get it out. Lavender sees Temerity struggle with his sword and yanks it out intact but bent. Temerity accepts the sword gracefully.

Theren gestures to Gage to scout ahead down the stone steps, which go winding and descending into the darkness. Gage, Temerity, Lavender and Theren proceed downwards in single file. Temerity seems oblivious to anything going on. Gage sees that the torch light is slowly changing in intensity. It is gradually becoming less natural, almost colder. Theren sees that the shadows are threatening the party, almost menacing them, so he whispers a warning to them about the shadows.

Temerity lights up Lavender’s sword to dispel some of the shadows and she raises her sword aloft. They see that the walls are made of stone – it is a rough-hewn basalt passageway. Theren hears a screech as the shadows pull back. They fight to get to the party but cannot enter the sphere of light created by Lavender’s glowing sword. The party walk for several minutes. All around them is the scent of decaying flesh invading their nostrils. There is no natural light at all in these depths.

The passageway begins to widen and the ground begins to flatten. They sense that their destination is close. Lavender is almost overwhelmed by a sense of undeath. She warns them all that there are undead down here. She now goes first with her lighted sword.

There is now a chamber beyond the end of the passageway in which Theren senses lots of necromantic magic. Lavender continues onwards; Gage notches an arrow to his bow in anticipation of danger.

There is a desk in the chamber to the side of what appears to be a normal wooden door. At the desk is a figure wearing tattered robes. It has half a face; the other half is a skull with a glowing green dot in the eye socket. Temerity addresses the figure and laments that they are lost, asking the way to the nearest pet shop. This confuses the figure. Temerity insists that they are lost but the figure is not convinced. Lavender shoves Temerity to one side and demands to be taken to Orris. The figure replies reverently that Orris is not taking visitors, so Lavender asks how to gain an audience. He says that they must come back in 3 days.

Lv asks the figure if Orris raised him. It replies that he was not fortunate enough to be raised by Orris’s hand. She asks if Orris is here in Arcadia. Temerity uses the opportunity to read its mind. The surface thoughts revolve around how to gain an audience with Orris, but Tm senses that there is something that it is guarding. Lavender leans forwards onto the desk, displaying the ring on her hand as she does, and stares him down, telling him that he would not do well do deny her. The zombie meets her glare and insists that it cannot disobey orders. Temerity reads its mind and sees that by breaking the rules, the zombie would suffer an eternity of torment. Lavender is getting angry and for an instant, she resembles Orris. The zombie is taken aback by this sudden link between its interrogator and its master. It bows to her and sends a message cantrip. A few minutes later, he asks them to come through.

Through the door is another cavern, filled with dark activities. It is like the antithesis of the cavern of the Displaced. The party sticks out and everyone pauses to watch them as they progress through the cavern. Theren looks up at them as he passes and sees different people and animals staring. He doesn’t like the attention and feels very uncomfortable. Conversely, Temerity basks in the attention. He taunts a goblin and it spits at him. A bugbear leads them through to a large, makeshift building at the end of the cavern. Inside is a small seating area where they are made to wait but they quickly lose track of time. After a significant amount of time, a person steps out of the door. It is a person with a familiar face…

**Day 12 (continued)**

The figure has the same white blond hair as Lavender, which is flopped over his face. Lavender stands immediately. The newcomer nods and turns back into the office, leaving the door open. Lavender follows him straight away. Gage pulls up his hood and follows them both. Gage sees one of the guards move their hand towards their weapon as he enters the office. Theren also follows them, but is hesitant and nervous.

Temerity, however, stays behind outside the office. He begins systematically defacing the publications in the waiting room, turning them all into gnomes being rude with goats, whilst also providing a lookout. There are two guards in the room with him. One seems rather unintelligent and focused on his task of standing to attention. The other tells him not to draw on the magazines. Temerity argues his case but the guard is unconvinced. Temerity ceases drawing and uses his rapier to cut the magazines into the shape of origami gnomes. The guard derides his bent rapier, so Temerity insults the guard’s mother. The guard moves to punch him but trips over a chair, falls over and breaks his nose.

Temerity speaks to the fallen guard, referring to Lavender as his prospective bride and Orris as his future brother-in-law, telling the guard that he does not want to upset his boss. The guard is really not convinced that Temerity could ever marry Lavender, but does not want to get embroiled in another confrontation with Temerity, so simply confiscates the magazines and leaves. Temerity starts singing a song under his breath about incompetent necromancers whilst petting his menagerie. Aurius is hiding behind his legs, quaking, so Temerity reassures him.

Lavender chooses to ignore the commotion outside. She, Gage and Theren move into the office with Orris. One wall is a massive bookcase, green curtains hang across other walls and a massive desk with a quill and a half-written letter dominate the middle of the room. Orris asks about Temerity and Lavender says it is best if he stays outside. Orris asks Theren to close the door. Theren is nervous but acquiesces.

Orris asks Lavender how she is. She is taken aback and does not know what to do or say. Orris’s manner is genial and friendly. He compliments Lavender. Outside, Temerity casts zone of truth. Lavender and Gage detect the spell and now must tell the truth, whereas Theren and Orris are still able to lie and do not know that the spell has been cast.

Orris understands why Lv has sought him out and tells her that there is much that each must explain to the other. He confesses that he has missed her. This news hits her hard and she confesses the same. Orris looks at Gage, whom he had hired to track Lavender. He explains to her why he did it, that he wanted to keep an eye to keep her safe. He stops and cannot continue; he tells her that there are too many others around. He wants to meet in another city instead.

He sends a telepathic message to Lavender, telling her that they cannot speak here and that there are too many things going on that even the two of them are not aware of. She sends back the questions of when and where. In response, he pulls a sending stone from a desk drawer and sends back to use it when they reach Adalens. She takes the stone and packs it away safely. She tries to hug him and he envelopes her with his embrace for an extended moment.

Theren watches all this feeling quite uncomfortable. Gage is being stone-faced, like a guard. They both receive a message asking them to keep Lavender safe. Gage simply acknowledges the message, but Theren is taken aback and does not know how to react.

Orris pulls back and begins a façade of animosity towards them. Lavender kicks the door open and storms out. As she does, she receives one final message, telling her that he loves her.

Temerity is lounging outside with his animals. Lavender strides over and pulls Temerity up by his scruff, dragging him out of the room. Temerity makes a scurrilous remark about their first time, but she ignores him. She frogmarches the party out of the necromancers’ cavern, dragging Temerity the whole way up the stairs and out of the manor.

**Day 13**

Outside the manor, the sun is beginning to rise. The whole night has passed and they had not even realised. It is extremely cold now; the dead foliage is rimed with frost. As they leave the manor grounds, Gage sniffs the air and notices a dead stench getting stronger. Outside the estate, Temerity is dropped unceremoniously in the road, but he rolls gracefully and hops up. The smell of death is getting stronger as the approach the centre of town.

Gage sends a message to Theren about what he is sensing. Theren stretches his senses out to feel the magic and sees a dark aura ahead. He instantly calls Lavender and tells her that he feels dark magic ahead and that they should not go that way. Lavender replies that darkness does not intimidate her. Temerity also senses that there is something ahead of them. He asks Lavender if she trusts him. Theren answers no. Temerity ignores him and asks Lavender to close her eyes and point the way that they should go. Lavender does as he asks and feels that the central square contains a powerful feeling of the undead. The feeling is lesser in other directions, but Lavender tells everyone that they have a duty to the people of Arcadia to deal with the undead scourge.

Temerity proceeds to make an inspiring speech, referencing their previous adventures and, for some inexplicable reason, gnomes doing lewd things. As he orates, an illusory image of a forest gnome with a goliath reading a sex manual appears. The goliath gentle nibbles on the gnome’s ear and vignettes appear of the goliath and gnome doing every sex position imaginable. Everyone is vastly and bizarrely inspired by this and also incredibly aroused but they all manage to control themselves. Runcible, however, succumbs to the stimulating imagery and Theren feels the dragon shudder on his shoulder. His back is strangely wet.

Lavender moves into the town square. Five zombies, five skeletons and two corpse-raisers await them, spread out across the town square. Battle is joined.

One of the corpse-raisers fires magic missiles and hits Gage and Theren. The other fires magic missiles and hits Lavender and Temerity. The zombies all advance towards the party, with three of them arriving directly in front of the party immediately. One of them reaches Lavender and slams her, causing only minimal damage. Others reach Temerity and Gage. Temerity uses sacred flame on the zombie right in front of him and it screams in pain. Gage uses his rapier to strike the zombie right in front of him and causes ichor to ooze out of it. Lavender rages and fights back against the zombie in front of her, severing one of its arms, but it does not slow it down. However, a final slash takes out the zombie and it collapses. The skeletons begin their attack; three of them move forwards towards the party and the other two hold back and shoot arrows. One tries to hit Lavender but misses, a second slashes Theren and the third slashes Gage. The archers shoot at Temerity and Lavender; Temerity is hit and Lavender suffers a glancing blow from the arrows. Theren uses shatter on the group directly attacking the party, blasting three of the skeletons and one of the zombies into shrapnel, leaving only one zombie next to the party.

One of the corpse-raisers shoots a blast of green energy at Lavender, sapping her strength; he has cast ray of enfeeblement on her. The other corpse-raiser advances from the opposite side of the square and shoots magic missiles at Theren in retribution. A cry flashes out across the square, speaking of the necromancers’ desperation. The other two zombies join the third directly in front of the party. One swipes at Gage and misses, another one swipes at Theren and misses and the last swipes at Lavender and hits a glancing blow. Temerity uses sacred flame on the zombie attacking Theren, making it cry out in agony, and heals Theren for some of the damage he has taken. Gage moves forwards towards the two corpse-raisers and tries to slash one of them with his rapier, but it dodges. Lavender overcomes her fatigue to slash at the zombie attacking her, only causing moderate damage. She successfully shakes off the enfeeblement effects fully. The two skeletons are still at range and shoot arrows at Theren, but only one hits, causing minimal damage. Theren shatters the two corpse-raisers, who are now standing beside each other; however, the spell causes only some damage and nowhere near as much as it should have.

The corpse-raiser not engaged with Gage moves forwards past the gnome, who causes minimal damage to his enemy at it passes, and tries to strike Theren, but he fails. The other corpse-raiser strikes Gage, drawing life energy from his body and into his own. One of the remaining zombies doubles back to attack Gage and causes serious hurt to him. Another attacks Theren and fails and the last attacks Lv and fails also. Temerity is deeply concerned at Gage’s dreadful state and heals him. He then uses sacred flame on the zombie in front of him, causing it to burn but it remains upright. Gage disengages from the corpse-raiser and zombie that were attacking him and hides in the shadows on the edges of the square, blending indistinguishably with the stone of the buildings. Lavender attacks the zombie in front of her, bifurcating it completely with a single stroke. She charges past it towards the corpse-raiser that had been attacking Gage but does not manage to hit it. The skeletons stay at range and shoot arrows at Theren again in retribution for his destruction of their comrades earlier; only one manages to hit him, though. Theren uses agonising blast on the corpse-raiser in front of him and causes significant damage. Runcible finally recovers from earlier and joins the fight, stinging the corpse-raiser; he is now looking very badly wounded.

The corpse-raisers both drain life from Theren and Lavender respectively, healing themselves. The zombies attack Lavender and Theren. Lavender receives a glancing blow but Theren is not hit. Temerity heals Theren back to full health. Gage sneaks forwards to attack the corpse-raiser by Lavender, causing significant damage with his rapier. Lavender also attacks the corpse-raiser by her; her blade rimes with frost, light refracts off in a rainbow sheen. She stabs it through the chest and whips it out in a glorious arc of scintillating beauty, with frozen fragments of blood glittering in the air. The skeletons shoot at Lavender in retribution for killing the corpse-raiser, causing only minimal damage. Theren hits the remaining corpse-raiser with an agonising blast, causing significant damage. He also activates cloak of flies, which overpowers the corpse-raider in a hail of golden scarabs.

The zombies try to slam Lavender and Theren, but both miss. Temerity uses sacred flame against the zombie in front of him, immolating it completely. Gage returns to the wall to hide and shoots the final zombie with his bow from his stealth position; the arrow passes straight through the zombie and thuds into a barrel of mouldy ale on the far side of the square. The zombie falls and Guido rushes over to start drinking the mouldy ale. Lavender charges at the furthest skeleton, blasting the bones into dust and obliterating it in one hit. The final remaining skeleton turns to face Lavender and fires its bow at her, causing minimal damage. Theren uses agonising blast to turn the final skeleton to fragments.

As the battle concludes, they are all suddenly confused as to why they would be attacked here after just speaking to Orris and being allowed to leave the manor safely.
--- End of File: ./Campaigns/Campaign 1/Chronicles/Entry 18.md ---

--- File: ./Campaigns/Campaign 1/Chronicles/Entry 19.md ---

**Day 13 (continued)**

Temerity and Gage observe the remains of the necromancers in the square. They notice a symbol on the arms of the corpses. It is similar to one that they saw on the walls in the cavern beneath the mansion – a skull with diamond eyes. This symbol, however, is inverted and different colours – dark blue and green. Gage attempts to discern its meaning, but with little success.

The party agrees to return to the inn to rest. Gage notices necromantic energy around the inn but it is not out of ordinary, given where they are. They enter and Temerity summons the innkeeper to the bar. The innkeeper isn’t happy to see him again. Lavender and Theren promise that they will leave with Temerity after they have eaten, in an attempt to appease the innkeeper. They all take a moment to sit and rest.

Lavender is concerned that Orris set them up for the fight and mulls this issue to herself. Temerity pets his animals. Innkeeper brings a cold breakfast out – cheeses, bread, meats. Gage asks him about the child that they acquired herbs for. The innkeeper replies that they’re doing better but are not out of danger yet.

The party discusses options for the journey to Adalens. They decide that the best course of action is to head through Pinechill village to the town of Midward to try and get a caravan down to Onasea village, which has a quay.

They start the walk south as soon as possible, since it is a day and a half’s walk to Pinechill village.

**Day 14**

They enter Pinechill during early evening of the following day. Gage senses that something is off as they enter the village limits. He smells the smell that he detected during their fight the previous morning, but it’s not quite the same scent. Korako smells something strange, too – like death and life at the same time.

Chikatika begs for food, so Temerity sends her to Theren, who gives her some berries from his pack. Lavender, meanwhile, heads to buy some rations. A dark-skinned gnome with bright ginger hair and beard mans a stall. He says that a dark carriage passed through recently on its way south. He advises Lavender to speak to a couple of village gossips about it.

Temerity notices a town-crier’s stage in the village square, so he performs to the crowd and the menagerie engages the children in the village. Gage and Theren watch the performance from nearby. The party decide to stay in the village for the night. During the performance, Gage focuses on creating the clockwork rabbit that he promised Temerity. The crowd finally begins to disperse.

Lavender discusses staying at the inn with the innkeeper, including a meal. The innkeeper makes a wager with Gage that he will be unable to eat a full adult-sized meal. The innkeeper retreats to the kitchen to fetch dinner.

Temerity starts performing in the corner of the room. The party notices a figure in another corner. Gage sees an aura around the figure. He reads their surface thoughts and picks up worry and a desire to stay hidden. Gage hints to Theren that they should meet this figure. Theren suggests to Chikatika that she introduce herself innocuously to the figure; however, he gives no reaction to her presence. Gage sends the figure a telepathic message, but again there is very little reaction.

Theren asks the innkeeper about the figure, but he says he knows very little, just that he paid handsomely for a room and has since kept to himself. The innkeeper places the food before them. Gage manages to eat around three quarters of the food but then struggles to finish. Temerity casts darkness as Chikatika sidles up, hoping for food. Gage tries to sweep the food to her, but it goes badly wrong, landing on her head instead. Gage starts blaming her loudly for interfering in his wager, whilst sending her telepathic messages to reassure her that he’s only acting.

The darkness dispels and the figure in the corner is now standing with an ornate knife in their hand, seemingly defensively. The innkeeper is outraged. Lavender manages to diffuse the situation and she, Gage and Theren head up to their rooms. Lavender shares with Theren, as she doesn’t trust Temerity.

Temerity stays in the bar arguing with the innkeeper, who is trying to throw him out. Temerity simply begins playing again, which somehow appeases the innkeeper. Gage climbs out of his window and watches the front door, awaiting the mysterious figure, in case he tries to leave. Temerity continues to play as the patrons drift away. The figure eventually heads upstairs. Temerity heads up almost immediately afterwards. Gage hears the music stop and calls it a night.

Temerity bribes Guido to poke his head into the stranger’s room. Guido approaches the room and half-squeezes under the door before becoming stuck. He returns to Temerity’s room just under 10 minutes later. He babbles about the figure removing its hood and it was glowing with a silvery glow and it had long white hair and sparkles coming out of its hands. Temerity immediately concludes that this person is a star descended to earth. He praises Guido and gives him beer. Temerity wakes Gage and heads next door to awaken Lavender and Theren.

Lavender wakes when she hears Temerity at the door. They argue over whether or not there is a star fallen to earth. She peeks through the keyhole and sees a radiant light. She sends the others to their rooms. Gage and Theren comply immediately. Temerity argues but she persuades him. Once alone, she knocks firmly on the door, which opens a crack.

Lavender smiles and apologises for the interruption. She speaks respectfully to him and mentions the name of Auriel and the oath that she took. He invites her in, since she is alone. The figure removes its cloak, revealing cold, radiant light. The figure is taller than Lavender, with glowing white skin and hair. Its eyes are deep blue with flecks of white in. It is ethereally beautiful and clearly not quite human.

The figure reveals that they are the offspring of Auriel – an aasimar. Their name is Anaphel. They reveal that they are here because they heard of the necromancers in the area and were sent by Auriel to investigate, since the cold regions are the demesne of Auriel. Lavender informs them that Arcadia is now a bastion of the necromancers. She states that the party is heading to Adalens to try and remove the head of the snake. Anaphel states that the forgotten temples and lost followers of Auriel are no coincidence. She tells them of the restored altar in the temple to the north-west of Mightrest. She offers their allegiance. She mentions that Orris is a high-ranking necromancer but she is unsure of his true loyalties. Anaphel bestows a blessing upon her. Lavender calls Theren across to Temerity and Gage’s room and explains to everyone about Anaphel and how they will be joining the group for now.

**Day 15**

The party rises the following morning feeling refreshed. Anaphel, recloaked, joins them for breakfast. Temerity still insists that Anaphel is a star. Theren is stunned into silence by the aasimar’s presence. No caravans seem to be heading south, so the party resigns itself to having to walk. Theren wants to speak to Anaphel but cannot seem to find the words. The day’s walk is uneventful.

During that evening, around the campfire, everyone is very settled and calm. Theren begins thinking of home. Lavender feels the compulsion to pray. Gage simply enjoys being in nature, as does Temerity. Finally, Temerity wanders over to Anaphel and present Korako to them.
--- End of File: ./Campaigns/Campaign 1/Chronicles/Entry 19.md ---
